#PROJECT
PR:PROJECT_TITLE                 	Identification of novel myokines
PR:PROJECT_TYPE                  	MS study
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	Skeletal myotubes release certain factors called myokines following exercise
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	that signal to other tissues including adipose, liver or the heart. These
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	myokines may promote the health benefits of exercise.
PR:INSTITUTE                     	Sanford-Burnham Medical Research Institute
PR:DEPARTMENT                    	Cardiovascular Pathobiology
PR:LAST_NAME                     	Vega
PR:FIRST_NAME                    	Rick
PR:ADDRESS                       	--
PR:EMAIL                         	rvega@sanfordburnham.org
PR:PHONE                         	--
#STUDY
ST:STUDY_TITLE                   	Mouse skeletal myotube chronic low-frequency stimulation
ST:STUDY_TYPE                    	Electrical stimulation
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	Cell culture media is collected from mouse myotubes subject to electrical
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	stimulation and control cells with no stimulation.
ST:INSTITUTE                     	SECIM
ST:LAST_NAME                     	Vega

#COLLECTION
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	Conditioned media was collected from the cell culture dish, and centrifuged at
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	3000xg, 4¡C for 10 min to remove cell debris. The supernatant was transferred
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	into new tube and stored at -80¡C. For the metabolomics analysis, 500 uL of
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	samples was put into 1.5 mL tube.
CO:SAMPLE_TYPE                   	Cells
#TREATMENT
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	Primary mouse myocytes were differentiated into myotubes for 3 days, and
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	electrically stimulated at 2.5V, 1.0 Hz by C-PAGE EP (Ionoptix). Conditioned
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	media was collected every 24 hr of stimulation. Conditioned media from the cells
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	without electrical stimulation was also collected as a negative control.

SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	see Sample Preparation of Cell Lysates.pdf

#CHROMATOGRAPHY

CH:INSTRUMENT_NAME            	Thermo Scientific-Dionex Ultimate 3000:
CH:COLUMN_NAME                	ACE Excel 2 C18-PFP Column (100 x 2.1mm) 2.0 µm
CH:CHROMATOGRAPHY_COMMENTS    	UHPLC, Thermo Scientific-Dionex Ultimate 3000: While setting up sequence, ensure
CH:CHROMATOGRAPHY_COMMENTS    	that method to be utilized is PFP-metabolomics-neg350-NoBuffer-0-SID and
CH:CHROMATOGRAPHY_COMMENTS    	PFP-metabolomics-neg-350-dd-MS2 for negative sequences. For positive sequences
CH:CHROMATOGRAPHY_COMMENTS    	utilize PFP-metabolomics-pos-350-0-SID and PFP-metabolomics-pos-350-dd-MS2.
CH:CHROMATOGRAPHY_COMMENTS    	Check the lines for air bubbles and purge line if present. Set injection volume
CH:CHROMATOGRAPHY_COMMENTS    	to 2uL for positive samples and 4uL for negative samples.
